## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TB
Start([POST validation]) --> CheckId{trip_leg.id is not None?}
CheckId -- Yes --> ErrSetUuid[/"ValidationError: Cannot set uuid when creating an object"/]
CheckId -- No --> RequiredChecks[/"Collect missing_fields and invalid_values"/]
RequiredChecks --> CheckDelivery{"delivery_type empty or in ['attended','unattended']?"}
CheckDelivery -- No --> AddInvalidDelivery([Add invalid: delivery_type must be 'attended' or 'unattended'])
CheckDelivery -- Yes --> CheckStatus{"status empty or in ['ACTIVE','INACTIVE','DELETED']?"}
AddInvalidDelivery --> CheckStatus
CheckStatus -- No --> AddInvalidStatus([Add invalid: status must be one of ACTIVE, INACTIVE, DELETED])
CheckStatus -- Yes --> CheckType{"type in ['PLANNED','ACTUAL']?"}
AddInvalidStatus --> CheckType
CheckType -- No --> AddInvalidType([Add invalid: type must be either PLANNED or ACTUAL])
CheckType -- Yes --> TypeBranch{"type == 'ACTUAL' or 'PLANNED'?"}
TypeBranch -- ACTUAL --> CheckCreatorShipment{"creator_shipment_id present?"}
TypeBranch -- PLANNED --> CheckShipmentNumber{"shipment_number present?"}
CheckCreatorShipment -- No --> AddMissingCreator([Add missing: CREATOR_SHIPMENT_ID])
CheckCreatorShipment -- Yes --> EvaluateErrors
CheckShipmentNumber -- No --> AddMissingShipment([Add missing: SHIPMENT_NUMBER])
CheckShipmentNumber -- Yes --> EvaluateErrors
AddMissingCreator --> EvaluateErrors
AddMissingShipment --> EvaluateErrors
AddInvalidType --> EvaluateErrors
EvaluateErrors{missing_fields or invalid_values exist?} -- Yes --> RaiseErrors[/"ValidationError: Missing required fields or Invalid values"/]
EvaluateErrors -- No --> Success([Validation passed])
```
